== National poll results ==
Poll results are listed in the table below in reverse chronological order. The highest percentage figure in each poll is displayed in bold, and its background is shaded in the leading party's colour. The "lead" column shows the [[percentage point]] difference between the two parties with the highest figures. When a poll result is a tie, the figures with the highest percentages are shaded and displayed in bold.

Most opinion polls do not cover [[Northern Ireland]], which has [[List of political parties in Northern Ireland|different major political parties]] to the rest of the United Kingdom. This distinction is made in the table below in the area column, where "GB" means [[Great Britain]], the island which contains England, Scotland and Wales and excludes Northern Ireland, and "UK" means [[United Kingdom]], which includes Northern Ireland. [[Plaid Cymru]] only stand candidates in [[Wales]] and [[Scottish National Party|the SNP]] only stand candidates in [[Scotland]]. The parties with the greatest numbers of votes in the [[2019 United Kingdom general election|2019 general election]] are listed here. Other parties are listed in the "Others" column.
